TL;DR: 本文研究了同时满足两个差分隐私约束的机制组合，提出了隐私区域的精确表示方法，并将其推广到任意数量DP约束的组合，最后应用于近似f-DP组合。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究同时满足多个差分隐私约束的机制组合问题，为复杂的隐私保护场景提供理论基础，解决现有方法在处理异构DP保证机制组合时的局限性。

Method: 通过二元假设检验的混合结构引理，推导出隐私区域的精确表示，将其表示为异构DP保证机制的混合组合，并推广到任意数量DP约束的组合。

Result: 建立了同时满足两个DP约束的机制组合的精确表示框架，证明了该框架可自然推广到任意数量DP约束，并成功应用于近似f-DP组合问题。

Conclusion: 提出的混合组合框架为多约束差分隐私机制组合提供了精确的理论基础，扩展了差分隐私组合理论的应用范围，特别是在处理异构隐私保证和近似f-DP方面具有重要价值。

Abstract: The exact composition of mechanisms for which two differential privacy (DP) constraints hold simultaneously is studied. The resulting privacy region admits an exact representation as a mixture over compositions of mechanisms of heterogeneous DP guarantees, yielding a framework that naturally generalizes to the composition of mechanisms for which any number of DP constraints hold. This result is shown through a structural lemma for mixtures of binary hypothesis tests. Lastly, the developed methodology is applied to approximate $f$-DP composition.

### [285] [Probability of super-regular matrices and MDS codes over finite fields](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.20983)
*Rathinakumar Appuswamy,Marco Bazzani,Spencer Congero,Joseph Connelly,Matthew Ekaireb,Kenneth Zeger*

Main category: cs.IT

TL;DR: 该论文证明了随机线性码为MDS码的概率阈值现象，并推导出随机矩阵为超正则矩阵的概率阈值，同时给出了几种渐近概率的精确表达式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究随机线性码成为最大距离可分(MDS)码的概率阈值行为，以及随机矩阵成为超正则矩阵的概率阈值，为理解这些重要代数结构的随机性质提供理论依据。

Method: 采用概率论和组合数学方法，分析随机线性码和随机矩阵的性质。通过渐近分析证明阈值现象，使用计数技术计算特定情况下的超正则矩阵数量。

Result: 1. 证明了随机线性码为MDS码的概率阈值：当$\frac{1}{q}\binom{n}{k} \to 0$时概率趋于1，当$\frac{1}{q}\binom{n}{k} \to \infty$时概率趋于0；2. 推导出随机矩阵为超正则矩阵的类似阈值；3. 得到了几种中间情形的精确渐近概率表达式；4. 发现4×4超正则矩阵数量不是多项式。

Conclusion: 随机线性码的MDS性质存在明确的概率阈值，这一阈值现象也适用于随机矩阵的超正则性质。这些结果为理解代数结构的随机行为提供了重要理论框架，并揭示了超正则矩阵计数问题的复杂性。

Abstract: Let $C$ be an $[n, k]$ linear code chosen uniformly at random over a finite field $\mathbb{F}_q$ of size $q$. The following asymptotic probability of $C$ being maximum distance separable (MDS) as $q,n,k\to\infty$ is known: If $\frac{1}{q}\binom{n}{k} \to 0$, then $P(C\text{ is MDS}) \to 1$. We demonstrate that this growth rate is in fact a threshold by proving: If $\frac{1}{q}\binom{n}{k} \to \infty$, then $P(C\text{ is MDS}) \to 0$. A matrix is (\textit{contiguous}) \textit{super-regular} if all of its (contiguous) square submatrices are nonsingular. The above results imply that for any $k \times k$ matrix $A$ chosen uniformly at random over $\mathbb{F}_q$, the following hold: If $\frac{4^k/\sqrt{k}}{q} \to 0$, then $P(A \text{ is super-regular}) \to 1$. If $\frac{4^k/\sqrt{k}}{q} \to \infty$, then $P(A \text{ is super-regular}) \to 0$. We also obtain the following asymptotic probabilities for two variations of the above questions: If $\frac{1}{q}\binom{n}{k} \to λ\in (0,\infty)$ and $k/n \to 0$, then $P(C\text{ is MDS}) \to e^{-λ}$. If $\frac{k^3/3}{q} \to λ\in (0,\infty)$, then $P(A \text{ is contiguous super-regular}) \to e^{-λ}$. The number of contiguous super-regular $3 \times 3$ matrices is also a polynomial. Finally, for $4 \times 4$ matrices, we show that the number of super-regular matrices is not a polynomial, nor even a quasi-polynomial of period less than 7, whereas our experimental evidence suggests that the number of contiguous super-regular matrices is a polynomial.

</details>

Abstract: We theoretically explain how multipath interference resizes PAM-4 constellation in the coherent regime and thus increases bit error rate fluctuation in intra data centers for the first time.

### [287] [Dual Representation of Minimum Divergence Under Integral Constraints](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.21027)
*Shubhanshu Shekhar,Shubhada Agrawal*

Main category: cs.IT

TL;DR: 提出一种两阶段方法，用于推导[0,1]^K上分布的最小散度问题的对偶表示，扩展了现有方法到更广泛的f-散度和积分约束，并应用于序列推断、估计和变化检测问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 统计学和概率论中的最小散度问题在积分约束下广泛出现于序列推断、多臂赌博机理论和分布鲁棒优化等领域。对偶表示是将信息论下界转化为可计算（通常接近最优）算法的关键步骤。现有方法主要针对相对熵和均值约束，需要扩展到更广泛的散度度量和约束类型。

Method: 提出两阶段方法：第一阶段使用有限维凸对偶技术推导有限支撑分布的对偶表示；第二阶段建立抽象交换论证，将离散化对偶提升到任意分布。从均值约束的最小相对熵（KL_inf）开始，将单维方法推广到任意维度，然后扩展到广泛的f-散度和一般积分约束泛函。

Result: 成功推导了[0,1]^K上分布的最小散度问题的对偶表示，覆盖了广泛的f-散度类型和一般积分约束。这些对偶表示能够将信息论下界转化为可计算的算法。通过构造[0,1]^K上观测的序列测试、估计和变化检测的最优程序，展示了结果的统计应用价值。

Conclusion: 提出的两阶段方法为推导约束最小散度问题的对偶表示提供了通用框架，显著扩展了现有技术的适用范围。该方法不仅理论上有价值，而且能够构造实际统计问题的最优程序，在序列推断、估计和变化检测等领域具有重要应用前景。

Abstract: Minimum divergence problems under integral constraints appear throughout statistics and probability, including sequential inference, bandit theory, and distributionally robust optimization. In many such settings, dual representations are the key step that convert information-theoretic lower bounds into computationally tractable (and often near-optimal) algorithms. In this paper, we present a general two-stage recipe for deriving dual representations of constrained minimum divergence (in the second argument) for distributions supported on $[0,1]^K$. The first stage derives a dual representation for finitely-supported distributions using classical finite-dimensional convex duality techniques, while the second establishes an abstract interchange argument that lifts this discretized dual to arbitrary distributions.
  We begin with the simplest case of mean-constrained minimum relative entropy, commonly called $\mathrm{KL}_{\inf}$, and generalize an existing argument from multi-armed bandits literature for $K=1$ to arbitrary dimensions. Our main contribution is to significantly expand the scope of this approach to a broad class of $f$-divergences (beyond relative entropy) and to general integral constraint functionals (beyond the mean constraint). Finally, we illustrate the statistical implications of our results by constructing optimal procedures for sequential testing, estimation, and change detection with observations in $[0,1]^K$.

</details>


### [288] [On generalized covering radii of binary primitive double-error-correcting BCH codes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.21068)
*Maosheng Xiong,Chi Hoi Yip*

Main category: cs.IT

TL;DR: 本文提出了广义超码引理来简化二进制原始双纠错BCH码的广义覆盖半径分析，建立了ρ₄的新下界，并证明了对于足够大的m，ρₖ(BCH(2,m))满足2k ≤ ρₖ ≤ 2k+1。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 二进制原始双纠错BCH码(BCH(2,m))的广义覆盖半径(GCR)是经典覆盖半径的高维扩展。虽然第二和第三GCR最近已被确定，但其证明依赖于高度复杂的组合论证，且对于更大阶数k的GCR层次结构行为仍基本未知。需要更系统的方法来研究GCR。

Method: 1. 引入广义超码引理，通过适当超码的广义汉明权来下界码的GCR。2. 应用该引理简化已知的ρ₂和ρ₃下界证明。3. 建立ρ₄的新下界。4. 结合组合论证和Weil型指数和估计，研究一般k的GCR层次结构。

Result: 1. 显著简化和简化了ρ₂(BCH(2,m))和ρ₃(BCH(2,m))已知下界的证明。2. 建立了ρ₄(BCH(2,m))的新下界。3. 证明了当m相对于k足够大时，2k ≤ ρₖ(BCH(2,m)) ≤ 2k+1，揭示了GCR层次结构的渐近行为。

Conclusion: 广义超码引理为研究线性码的广义覆盖半径提供了有力的新工具，不仅简化了现有结果，还使得探索更高阶GCR成为可能。对于BCH(2,m)码，GCR层次结构在渐近意义下表现出线性增长特性，为理解这类重要码的覆盖性质提供了新见解。

Abstract: The generalized covering radii (GCR) of linear codes are a fundamental higher-dimensional extension of the classical covering radius. While the second and third GCR of binary primitive double-error-correcting BCH codes, $\text{BCH}(2,m)$, were recently determined, their proofs relied on highly complex combinatorial arguments, and the behavior of the GCR hierarchy for larger orders $k$ has remained largely unexplored. In this paper, we introduce the Generalized Supercode Lemma, which lower-bounds the GCR of a code using the generalized Hamming weights of an appropriate supercode. Applying this lemma, we significantly streamline and simplify the proofs for the known lower bounds of $ρ_2(\text{BCH}(2,m))$ and $ρ_3(\text{BCH}(2,m))$, and we establish a new lower bound for $ρ_4(\text{BCH}(2,m))$. Furthermore, by combining combinatorial arguments with Weil-type exponential sum estimates, we investigate the GCR hierarchy for general $k$, proving that $2k \le ρ_k(\text{BCH}(2,m)) \le 2k+1$ whenever $m$ is sufficiently large compared to $k$.

</details>


### [289] [Anchored Likelihood-Ratio Geometry of Anonymous Shuffle Experiments: Exact Privacy Envelopes and Universal Low-Budget Design](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.21197)
*Alex Shvets*

Main category: cs.IT

TL;DR: 该论文提出了匿名洗牌实验的几何框架，基于锚定仿射似然比定律，研究了隐私保护机制的最优设计问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究匿名洗牌实验中的隐私保护机制设计，旨在在满足局部差分隐私约束下，找到最优的随机响应机制，以最大化统计效用同时保护用户隐私。

Method: 建立基于锚定仿射似然比定律的几何框架，将有限输出d元信道与锚定定律对应；采用凸f-散度和曲棍球轮廓分析隐私保护性能；在成对χ*预算下证明精确迹容量和双轨道前沿定理。

Result: 1) 在所有ε₀-LDP信道中，二元随机响应在洗牌后普遍极值化所有凸f-散度和曲棍球轮廓；2) 刚性逆定理表明有限n时两个定向包络的饱和强制二元端点定律；3) 在低预算机制下，增强随机响应在所有信道和估计器中达到极小极大最优的尖锐常数；4) 在原始LDP容量约束下，问题简化为具有明确最优子集大小的子集选择。

Conclusion: 该论文为匿名洗牌实验提供了系统的几何框架，建立了隐私保护机制设计的基本理论，证明了二元随机响应在特定条件下的最优性，并为实际应用提供了可计算的最优设计方法。

Abstract: We develop a geometric framework for anonymous shuffle experiments based on an anchored affine likelihood-ratio law: a mean-zero measure on the regular simplex polytope. Every finite-output d-ary channel corresponds, up to refinements, to a unique anchored law, and conversely. On privacy: among all epsilon_0-LDP channels, binary randomized response universally extremizes all convex f-divergences and hockey-stick profiles after shuffling. A rigidity converse shows that saturation of both directed envelopes at finite n forces the binary endpoint law. On design: under the pairwise chi_* budget, we prove exact trace-cap and two-orbit frontier theorems. Every frontier point is realized by a mixture of at most two orbit laws. In the low-budget regime, augmented randomized response is minimax-optimal to the sharp constant over all channels and estimators. Under the raw LDP cap, the problem reduces to subset-selection with explicit optimal subset size. The arguments are self-contained and independent of the author's trilogy.

</details>


### [290] [A Constructive Approach to $q$-Gaussian Distributions: $α$-Divergence as Rate Function and Generalized de Moivre-Laplace Theorem](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.21391)
*Hiroki Suyari,Antonio M. Scarfone*

Main category: cs.IT

TL;DR: 该论文为幂律分布建立了一个构造性概率框架，从非线性微分方程dy/dx = y^q出发，推导出广义二项分布，证明了在0<q<1时的LDP（速率函数为α-散度），并建立了广义de Moivre-Laplace定理，显示该分布收敛到q-高斯分布。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 虽然大偏差原理和中心极限定理在i.i.d.假设下已有完善表述，但幂律分布的概率基础主要通过描述性模型或变分原理发展，缺乏类似经典二项过程的构造性推导。本文旨在为幂律分布建立一个构造性概率框架。

Method: 从非线性微分方程dy/dx = y^q出发，不预先假设特定分布。建立代数和组合基础，推导出基于有限计数的广义二项分布。在0<q<1时证明该分布的LDP，识别α-散度为速率函数。证明广义de Moivre-Laplace定理，显示分布收敛到q-高斯分布。

Result: 证明了广义二项分布在0<q<1时的LDP，速率函数为α-散度；对于更重的尾部(q>1)，宏观标度会失效。证明了广义de Moivre-Laplace定理，显示分布收敛到q-高斯分布，标度律遵循n^{q/2}阶。数值验证了q∈(0,2)不同值的结果。

Conclusion: 该框架为幂律分布提供了构造性基础，统一了平移不变指数族和重标度不变幂律族。将构造性框架与信息几何结构联系起来，揭示了非线性导致的标度律n^{q/2}。

Abstract: The Large Deviation Principle (LDP) and the Central Limit Theorem (CLT) are concepts of information theory and probability. While their formulations are established under the i.i.d. assumption, the probabilistic foundation for power-law distributions has primarily evolved through descriptive models or variational principles, rather than a constructive derivation comparable to the classical binomial process. This paper establishes a constructive probabilistic framework for power-law distributions, proceeding from the nonlinear differential equation $dy/dx = y^q$ without assuming a specific distribution a priori. We build the algebraic and combinatorial foundations, which lead to a generalized binomial distribution based on finite counting. We prove the LDP for this generalized binomial distribution in the regime $0 < q < 1$, demonstrating that the $α$-divergence is identified as the rate function, and clarify the breakdown of this macroscopic scaling for heavier tails ($q > 1$). This result connects our constructive framework to the structures of information geometry. Furthermore, we prove a generalized de Moivre-Laplace theorem, showing that the generalized binomial distribution converges to a heavy-tailed limit distribution (the $q$-Gaussian distribution). We derive that the scaling law follows the order of $n^{q/2}$ as a consequence of the underlying nonlinearity. These analytical results are numerically verified for distinct values of $q \in (0, 2)$. This framework provides a constructive basis that unifies the shift-invariant exponential family and the rescaling-invariant power-law family.

</details>


### [291] [Structure-aware divergences for comparing probability distributions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.22237)
*Rohit Sahasrabuddhe,Renaud Lambiotte*

Main category: cs.IT

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种考虑元素相似性结构的新型散度度量，相比传统信息论量（如KL散度）能更好地处理具有几何结构的数据。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 许多自然和社会科学系统包含具有相似关系的元素（如共享技能的职业或相似特征的物种），但传统信息论量（熵和f-散度）将这些元素视为可互换的，忽略了相似性结构。

Method: 引入了一族对底层域几何结构敏感的散度，这些散度是结构感知熵的Bregman散度，保留了Kullback-Leibler散度和Shannon熵的多个优点。

Result: 结构感知散度在合成聚类任务中能恢复传统散度遗漏的植入模式，计算速度比最优传输距离快几个数量级。在经济地理学和生态学应用中，该方法能根据不同的职业相关性概念产生不同的地理分布区域化，并复现了使用最优传输方法获得的生态学功能β多样性见解。

Conclusion: 提出的结构感知散度为处理具有相似性结构的数据提供了有效的框架，在计算效率和模式识别能力方面优于传统方法，在多个科学领域具有应用价值。

Abstract: Many natural and social science systems are described using probability distributions over elements that are related to each other: for instance, occupations with shared skills or species with similar traits. Standard information theory quantities such as entropies and $f$-divergences treat elements interchangeably and are blind to the similarity structure. We introduce a family of divergences that are sensitive to the geometry of the underlying domain. By virtue of being the Bregman divergences of structure-aware entropies, they provide a framework that retains several advantages of Kullback-Leibler divergence and Shannon entropy. Structure-aware divergences recover planted patterns in a synthetic clustering task that conventional divergences miss and are orders of magnitude faster than optimal transport distances. We demonstrate their applicability in economic geography and ecology, where structure plays an important role. Modelling different notions of occupation relatedness yields qualitatively different regionalisations of their geographic distribution. Our methods also reproduce established insights into functional $β$-diversity in ecology obtained with optimal transport methods.

</details>

### [292] [Developing an ESG-Oriented Large Language Model through ESG Practices](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.20480)
*Gabriel Assis,Ayrton Surica,Pedro Kroll,Gabriela Aires,Darian Rabbani,Edson Bollis,Lucas Pellicer,Aline Paes*

Main category: cs.CE

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种面向ESG的LLM适配管道，通过LoRA和IRM等参数高效方法对Qwen-3-4B进行ESG专业化适配，在生成式ESG问答任务中表现优于原始模型和基线模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前LLM在ESG金融领域的应用主要集中于分类、评分等判别式任务，对需要领域知识和上下文理解的交互式生成式ESG场景支持有限。需要开发能够整合ESG原则作为指导约束的LLM适配方法。

Result: ESG适配模型在生成、语义、可读性和环境影响等多维度指标上一致优于原始Qwen-3-4B模型以及Llama-3、Gemma-3等竞争基线。尽管工具知识集成仍存在局限，但模型在ESG领域表现出色。

Abstract: Environmental, Social, and Governance (ESG) considerations play a central role in contemporary financial decision-making. In parallel, Large Language Model (LLM) applications in this domain have primarily emphasized well-defined discriminative tasks, such as classification or scoring, which have proven effective for structured analysis and benchmarking. However, this prevailing focus offers limited support for more interactive and generative ESG scenarios, where embedded domain knowledge and contextual understanding are essential. In this work, we propose an ESG-oriented adaptation pipeline for LLMs that integrates ESG principles not only as a target domain, but also as guiding constraints throughout training and evaluation. Building on the Qwen-3-4B architecture, we explore parameter-efficient adaptation strategies using Low-Rank Adaptation (LoRA) and the Instruction-Residual Method (IRM) to produce three ESG-specialized models. We evaluate the proposed models on ESG question answering under both zero-shot and knowledge-augmented settings, using a diverse set of generative, semantic, readability, and environmental impact metrics. Our results show that the ESG-adapted models consistently outperform their original counterparts and competitive baselines such as Llama-3 and Gemma-3. Although limitations remain in tool-based knowledge integration, this work establishes a foundation for ESG-oriented language generation and highlights the importance of responsible, domain-aware LLM adaptation.

</details>


### [293] [CICDWOA: A Collective Cognitive Sharing Whale Optimization Algorithm with Cauchy Inverse Cumulative Distribution for 2D/3D Path Planning and Engineering Design Problems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.20501)
*Junhao Wei,Yanxiao Li,Seyedali Mirjalili,Dexing Yao,Yifu Zhao,Haochen Li,Xudong Ye,Zikun Li,Qingyang Xu,Baili Lu,Ngai Cheong,Dengcheng Yang,Sio-Kei Im,Yapeng Wang,Xu Yang*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: The Whale Optimization Algorithm (WOA) has shown strong optimization ability but still suffers from premature convergence and weak search diversity. To address these issues, this paper proposes an enhanced WOA variant called CICDWOA. The proposed algorithm introduces a Good Nodes Set (GNS) method for uniform population initialization, a Collective Cognitive Sharing (CCS) mechanism to enhance group collaboration, and an Enhanced Spiral Updating strategy based on the Cauchy Inverse Cumulative Distribution (CICD) to strengthen global exploration and local exploitation balance. In addition, a nonlinear convergence factor and a Hybrid Gaussian-Cauchy mutation based on Differential Evolution (DE) further improve convergence efficiency and population diversity. CICDWOA was evaluated on 23 benchmark functions, 2D robot path planning problems, 3D UAV path planning tasks and 10 engineering design problems. Statistical experiment results show that CICDWOA achieves faster convergence, higher accuracy, and better robustness than classical WOA and other advanced metaheuristic algorithms. CICDWOA gained average Friedman value of 1.6790, ranking first among the SOTA algorithms. And the results of engineering simulations confirm that CICDWOA provides an effective and general framework for solving complex optimization and engineering problems. The code of CICDWOA are available on \href{URL}{https://github.com/JunhaoWei-mpu/ROBIS-Lab/tree/CICDWOA}.

### [294] [ALL-FEM: Agentic Large Language models Fine-tuned for Finite Element Methods](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.21011)

Abstract: Finite element (FE) analysis guides the design and verification of nearly all manufactured objects. However, implementing FE codes and analyzing simulation results demands expertise across numerical analysis, continuum mechanics, and programming. Conventional Large Language Models (LLMs) can generate FE code, but they hallucinate, lack awareness of variational structures, and cannot close the loop from problem statement to a verified solution. Here, we propose ALL-FEM, an autonomous simulation system that integrates agentic AI with domain-specific, fine-tuned LLMs for FEniCS code generation across solid, fluid, and multiphysics applications. We construct a corpus of 1000+ verified FEniCS scripts by combining 500+ curated expert codes with a retrieval-augmented, multi-LLM pipeline that generates and filters codes for diverse PDEs, geometries, and boundary conditions. Our agentic framework orchestrates specialized agents, powered by fine-tuned LLMs, to formulate problems as PDEs, generate and debug code and visualize the results. By showing that relatively small, fine-tuned LLMs, orchestrated through agentic frameworks, can automate FE workflows, ALL-FEM offers a blueprint for autonomous simulation systems in computational science and engineering.

We apply cosine-similarity analysis to TabPFN-derived embeddings, visualise full posterior distributions from an iterative inference procedure, and compute SHAP-based feature importance, all without model retraining. Learned embeddings clearly separate Clay and Sand samples without explicit soil-type supervision; iterative imputation improves predictions for four of five target parameters, with posterior widths that reflect physically reasonable parameter-specific uncertainty; and SHAP analysis reveals the inter-parameter dependency structure, recovering established geotechnical relationships including the Skempton compression index correlation and the inverse dependence of preconsolidation pressure on water content. ### [296] [How Short Is Too Short? Power Analysis for BIC-Based Changepoint Detection in Ecological Monitorin](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.21154)
*Ang A. Li*

Main category: cs.CE

TL;DR: 针对生态时间序列的变点检测进行模拟功率分析，评估BIC-Binseg方法在不同序列长度、效应大小和变点数量下的检测能力，发现PELT方法在自相关数据中表现更优


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 生态时间序列通常较短（10-50个观测值），但变点检测方法在这些短序列中的统计功效很少被评估，需要为生态学家提供实用的检测指导

Method: 采用模拟功率分析，评估BIC-Binseg方法在108种组合（序列长度、效应大小、变点数量）下的表现；比较PELT方法在自相关数据中的性能；与早期预警信号（EWS）方差趋势测试对比；在珊瑚礁和沙漠啮齿动物时间序列上进行实证验证

Result: BIC-Binseg检测单个变点需要n≥30且效应大小≥2.0才能达到≥80%功效；检测2-3个变点需要n≥50且ES≥5.0；BIC方法保守，低估变点多于高估；AR(1)自相关（φ=0.6）使BIC-Binseg功效降低40%，但PELT在中等自相关下仍保持85-91%功效；EWS在ES<1.5时优于变点检测，但其检测率不随效应大小变化（约73%）

Conclusion: 生态学家应优先选择PELT而非Binseg-BIC处理自相关数据；应用变点分析前应计算预期效应大小；结果应结合置换检验；提供功率热图作为实用查找工具

Abstract: Changepoint detection is increasingly applied to ecological time series, yet statistical power at the short series lengths typical of monitoring (10-50 observations) is rarely assessed. We present a simulation-based power analysis for BIC-based Binary Segmentation across 108 combinations of series length, effect size, and number of changepoints. BIC achieves $\geq$80% power for a single changepoint only at $n \geq 30$ with effect size $\geq 2.0$; detecting 2-3 changepoints requires $n \geq 50$ and ES $\geq 5.0$. BIC is conservative, underestimating changepoints more often than overestimating. AR(1) autocorrelation ($φ= 0.6$) reduces BIC-Binseg power by 40%, but PELT with a standard penalty maintains 85-91% power even under moderate autocorrelation. Comparison with early warning signal (EWS) variance-trend tests reveals a crossover: at ES $< 1.5$, EWS outperforms changepoint detection, but EWS rates are invariant to effect size ($\sim$73%), suggesting noise detection rather than genuine signals. Cross-system empirical validation on coral reef (Moorea, $n = 18$) and desert rodent (Portal Project, $n = 49$) time series confirms that detection succeeds when effect sizes fall in the predicted "reliable" zone. We provide power heatmaps as practical lookup tools and recommend that ecologists prefer PELT over Binseg-BIC for autocorrelated data, compute expected effect sizes before applying changepoint analysis, and pair results with permutation tests.

### [297] [Hybrid Quantum-Classical Branch-and-Price for Intra-Day Electric Vehicle Charging Scheduling via Partition Coloring](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.21374)
*Peng Sun,Liang Zhong,Qing-Guo Zeng,Li Wang*

Main category: cs.CE

TL;DR: 论文提出了一种结合量子退火启发算法(QAIA)的分支定价算法，用于解决电动汽车充电调度问题，该问题被建模为分区着色问题(PCP)的变体。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 电动汽车在公共停车场和车队运营中的快速部署带来了具有挑战性的日内充电调度问题，这些问题受到充电器容量有限和车辆停留时间短的限制。传统方法在处理大规模和困难实例时面临计算效率瓶颈。

Method: 将EV充电调度问题建模为分区着色问题(PCP)的变体，设计分支定价算法：主问题选择可行的充电间隔组合，定价子问题为最大独立集问题。将子问题重新表述为二次无约束二进制优化(QUBO)模型，并使用MindQuantum框架中的量子退火启发算法(BSB和SimCIM)求解，主问题使用Gurobi求解。

Result: 在合成EV充电实例上的计算实验表明：QAIA增强算法在中小型实例上与纯Gurobi基准相当，在大型和困难实例上明显优于基准。在多个基准算法达到时间限制且存在非零最优性差距的情况下，基于QAIA的变体能够在相同时间预算内闭合差距并证明最优性。

Conclusion: 将量子退火启发算法集成到经典分解方案中，是大规模电动汽车充电调度及相关PCP应用的一个有前景的方向。

Abstract: The rapid deployment of electric vehicles (EVs) in public parking facilities and fleet operations raises challenging intra-day charging scheduling problems under tight charger capacity and limited dwell times. We model this problem as a variant of the Partition Coloring Problem (PCP), where each vehicle defines a partition, its candidate charging intervals are vertices, and temporal and resource conflicts are represented as edges in a conflict graph. On this basis, we design a branch-and-price algorithm in which the restricted master problem selects feasible combinations of intervals, and the pricing subproblem is a maximum independent set problem. The latter is reformulated as a quadratic unconstrained binary optimization (QUBO) model and solved by quantum-annealing-inspired algorithms (QAIA) implemented in the MindQuantum framework, specifically the ballistic simulated branching (BSB) and simulated coherent Ising machine (SimCIM) methods, while the master problem is solved by Gurobi. Computational experiments on a family of synthetic EV charging instances show that the QAIA-enhanced algorithms match the pure Gurobi-based branch-and-price baseline on small and medium instances, and clearly outperform it on large and hard instances. In several cases where the baseline reaches the time limit with non-zero optimality gaps, the QAIA-based variants close the gap and prove optimality within the same time budget. These results indicate that integrating QAIA into classical decomposition schemes are a promising direction for large-scale EV charging scheduling and related PCP applications.

</details>


### [298] [A coupled Aeroelastic-Flight Dynamic Framework for Free-Flying Flexible Aircraft with Gust Interactions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.21650)
*Nikolaos D. Tantaroudas,Andrea Da Ronch,Ilias Karachalios,Kenneth J. Badcock,Rafael Palacios*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为非常柔性飞机在阵风遭遇条件下的耦合气动弹性与飞行动力学分析提供一个完整、自包含的数学框架，解决现有工具在跨学科耦合建模方面的不足。

Method: 集成几何精确非线性梁理论（结构动力学）、基于Theodorsen薄翼理论的非定常二维条带气动力（考虑尾迹和阵风穿透效应）、以及基于四元数的刚体飞行动力学（无奇点姿态传播），将耦合系统组装成一阶状态空间形式。

Result: 框架通过已发布的基准测试验证，包括高空长航时飞机配置和非常柔性飞翼，在结构频率、颤振速度和静态气动弹性变形方面表现出良好一致性。

Conclusion: 该论文为研究人员实现非常柔性飞机的耦合气动弹性-飞行动力学分析工具提供了一个自包含的参考框架，支持时域仿真、模型降阶和控制设计。

Abstract: A complete, self-contained mathematical framework for modelling the coupled aeroelastic and flight dynamic behaviour of free-flying flexible aircraft subject to atmospheric gust encounters is presented. The framework integrates three physical disciplines: geometrically-exact nonlinear beam theory for structural dynamics, unsteady two-dimensional strip aerodynamics based on Theodorsen thin-aerofoil theory with indicial functions for shed-wake and gust-penetration effects, and quaternion-based rigid-body flight dynamics for singularity-free attitude propagation. The coupled system is assembled into a first-order state-space form amenable to time-domain simulation, model order reduction, and control design. Detailed derivations of all coupling terms, including coordinate transformations between aerodynamic and structural frames, the Jacobian block structure, and gust input matrices, are provided. Two gust models are treated: the certification-standard discrete gust and the Von Karman continuous turbulence spectrum. The framework is verified against published benchmarks, including high-altitude long-endurance aircraft configurations and a very flexible flying-wing, demonstrating close agreement in structural frequencies, flutter speed, and static aeroelastic deflections. This paper serves as a self-contained reference for researchers implementing coupled aeroelastic-flight dynamic analysis tools for very flexible aircraft.

### [299] [Cohesive phase-field fracture with an explicit strength surface: an eigenstrain-based return-mapping formulation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.21811)
*Tim Hageman*

Main category: cs.CE

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于本征应变的局部本构模型，用于模拟粘聚相场断裂，无需额外全局自由度，可直接集成到现有有限元代码中。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准相场断裂方法基于脆性断裂理论，无法规定材料强度用于裂纹成核，也难以捕捉粘聚断裂行为。现有的本征应变方法虽然克服了这些限制，但依赖于直接能量最小化框架而非标准有限元程序。

Method: 利用本征应变无需空间梯度的特性，将其重新表述为局部本构模型（类似于塑性模型），在每个积分点求解。考虑了两种强度准则：具有独立拉伸和剪切强度的非光滑准则，以及类似Drucker-Prager的光滑准则（捕捉压缩下的压力相关强化）。推导了两种准则的一致切线算子以确保全局牛顿-拉弗森求解器的稳健收敛。

Result: 通过三个基准问题验证：带孔板在拉伸和压缩下的响应、单边缺口板在剪切下的响应、缺口板在动态载荷下的响应。结果展示了网格无关性和相场长度尺度无关性，证实断裂能量控制脆性与粘聚状态之间的转变，并自然捕捉了动态载荷下的裂纹分叉等复杂现象。

Conclusion: 提出的基于本征应变的局部本构模型成功实现了粘聚相场断裂模拟，无需额外全局自由度，可直接集成到现有有限元代码中，为相场断裂方法提供了更实用和灵活的框架。

Abstract: Standard phase-field fracture methods are rooted in brittle fracture theory and therefore do not inherently prescribe a material strength for crack nucleation, while also struggling to capture cohesive fracture behaviour. Recent eigenstrain-based formulations overcome both limitations by introducing fracture eigenstrains that decouple the strength surface from the fracture energy, but their implementation has so far relied on direct energy-minimization frameworks rather than standard finite-element procedures. In this work, we exploit the fact that the eigenstrains require no spatial gradients and reformulate the eigenstrain evolution as a local constitutive model, analogous to those used in plasticity, that is resolved at each integration point. As a result, the cohesive phase-field requires no additional global degrees of freedom beyond those of a standard phase-field formulation and can be readily integrated into existing finite-element codes. Two strength criteria are considered: a non-smooth criterion with independent tensile and shear strengths, and a smooth Drucker-Prager-like criterion that captures pressure-dependent strengthening under compression. Consistent tangent operators are derived for both criteria, ensuring robust convergence of the global Newton-Raphson solver. The framework is validated against three benchmark problems: a plate with a hole under tension and compression, a single-edge notched plate under shear, and a notched plate under dynamic loading. The results demonstrate mesh-independent and phase-field length-scale-independent behaviour, confirm that the fracture energy governs the transition between brittle and cohesive regimes, and show that complex phenomena such as crack branching under dynamic loading are naturally captured. All source codes are openly available.

</details>

### [300] [SURF: Signature-Retained Fast Video Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.21002)
*Kaixin Ding,Xi Chen,Sihui Ji,Yuan Gao,Liang Hou,Xin Tao,Hengshuang Zhao*

Main category: cs.GR

TL;DR: SURF是一个高效的高分辨率视频生成框架，通过两阶段方法（预览+精炼）在保持原始模型特征的同时实现显著加速，可作为插件兼容多种基础模型和加速方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 高分辨率视频生成需求增长，但现有方法生成速度慢（如Wan2.1生成720p视频需50分钟以上），且现有加速方法大多会损害原始模型的布局、语义、运动等特征。

Method: 提出两阶段框架：1）预览阶段：在最优分辨率下推理并下采样潜在空间生成低分辨率预览，采用无训练的噪声重移技术缓解分辨率降低带来的特征损失；2）精炼阶段：设计Refiner上采样预览，建立预览与高分辨率目标的映射关系减少去噪步骤，集成移位窗口并精心设计训练范式。

Result: SURF实现了显著加速：为Wan 2.1生成5秒16fps 720p视频提供12.5倍加速，为HunyuanVideo生成5秒24fps 720p视频提供8.7倍加速，同时最大程度保持原始模型特征。

Conclusion: SURF是一个概念简单的高效高分辨率视频生成框架，可作为插件兼容多种基础模型和加速方法，在保持原始模型特征的同时大幅提升生成速度。

Abstract: The demand for high-resolution video generation is growing rapidly. However, the generation resolution is severely constrained by slow inference speeds. For instance, Wan2.1 requires over 50 minutes to generate a single 720p video. While previous works explore accelerating video generation from various aspects, most of them compromise the distinctive signatures (e.g., layout, semantic, motion) of the original model. In this work, we propose SURF, an efficient framework for generating high-resolution videos, while maximally keeping the signatures. Specifically, SURF divides video generation into two stages: First, we leverage the pretrained model to infer at optimal resolution and downsample latent to generate low-resolution previews in fast speed; then we design a Refiner to upscale the preview. In the preview stage, we identify that directly inferring a model (trained with higher resolution) on lower resolution causes severe losses in signatures. So we introduce noise reshifting, a training-free technique that mitigates this issue by conducting initial denoising steps on the original resolution and switching to low resolution in later steps. In the refine stage, we establish a mapping relationship between the preview and the high-resolution target, which significantly reduces the denoising steps. We further integrate shifting windows and carefully design the training paradigm to get a powerful and efficient Refiner. In this way, SURF enables generating high-resolution videos efficiently while maximally closer to the signatures of the given pretrained model. SURF is conceptually simple and could serve as a plug-in that is compatible with various base model and acceleration methods. For example, it achieves 12.5x speedup for generating 5-second, 16fps, 720p Wan 2.1 videos and 8.7x speedup for generating 5-second, 24fps, 720p HunyuanVideo.

</details>


### [301] [MineRobot: A Unified Framework for Kinematics Modeling and Solving of Underground Mining Robots in Virtual Environments](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.22055)
*Shengzhe Hou,Xinming Lu,Tianyu Zhang,Changqing Yan,Xingli Zhang*

Main category: cs.GR

TL;DR: MineRobot：一个用于地下采矿机器人运动学建模与求解的统一框架，通过拓扑处理将闭链机构转换为独立路径，实现实时正向和逆向运动学计算


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 地下采矿机器人在虚拟环境中用于训练、规划和数字孪生应用，需要可靠的运动学模型以避免危险的实际试验。采矿机器人通常是闭链机构（线性驱动器和平面四杆机构），这使得运动学建模和实时求解具有挑战性，需要避免机器人特定的手动推导

Method: 1. 引入采矿机器人描述格式（MRDF），用于参数化采矿机器人运动学，具有执行器和闭环约束的原生语义；2. 开发拓扑处理流程，将四杆子结构收缩为广义关节，并为每个执行器提取独立拓扑等效路径（ITEP），分类为四种规范类型；3. 利用ITEP独立性，将每类求解器组合成以执行器为中心的序列正向运动学管道；4. 基于相同分解，将逆向运动学公式化为边界约束优化问题，采用交替更新执行器长度的Gauss-Seidel风格程序求解

Result: 实验表明，MineRobot通过将耦合的闭环运动学转换为一系列小型拓扑感知求解，提供了虚拟环境应用所需的实时性能和鲁棒性

Conclusion: MineRobot框架避免了机器人特定的手动推导，支持高效计算，能够满足虚拟环境应用对实时性能和鲁棒性的要求，为地下采矿机器人的运动学建模和求解提供了统一的解决方案

Abstract: Underground mining robots are increasingly operated in virtual environments (VEs) for training, planning, and digital-twin applications, where reliable kinematics is essential for avoiding hazardous in-situ trials. Unlike typical open-chain industrial manipulators, mining robots are often closed-chain mechanisms driven by linear actuators and involving planar four-bar linkages, which makes both kinematics modeling and real-time solving challenging. We present \emph{MineRobot}, a unified framework for modeling and solving the kinematics of underground mining robots in VEs. First, we introduce the Mining Robot Description Format (MRDF), a domain-specific representation that parameterizes kinematics for mining robots with native semantics for actuators and loop closures. Second, we develop a topology-processing pipeline that contracts four-bar substructures into generalized joints and, for each actuator, extracts an Independent Topologically Equivalent Path (ITEP), which is classified into one of four canonical types. Third, leveraging ITEP independence, we compose per-type solvers into an actuator-centered sequential forward-kinematics (FK) pipeline. Building on the same decomposition, we formulate inverse kinematics (IK) as a bound-constrained optimization problem and solve it with a Gauss--Seidel-style procedure that alternates actuator-length updates. By converting coupled closed-loop kinematics into a sequence of small topology-aware solves, the framework avoids robot-specific hand derivations and supports efficient computation. Experiments demonstrate that MineRobot provides the real-time performance and robustness required by VE applications.

</details>
